  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_aac2d710-c7b8-479c-b878-799214dcaab7'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer3066025266237448749">Moving to a space station at the edge of the galaxy was always going to be the death of Hanna’s social life. Nobody said it might actually get her killed.<br/><br/>The sci-fi saga that began with the breakout bestseller <i>Illuminae</i> continues on board the Jump Station <i>Heimdall</i>, where two new characters will confront the next wave of the BeiTech assault.<br/><br/>Hanna is the station captain’s pa</span>
  <span id="freeText3066025266237448749" style="display:none">Moving to a space station at the edge of the galaxy was always going to be the death of Hanna’s social life. Nobody said it might actually get her killed.<br /><br />The sci-fi saga that began with the breakout bestseller <i>Illuminae</i> continues on board the Jump Station <i>Heimdall</i>, where two new characters will confront the next wave of the BeiTech assault.<br /><br />Hanna is the station captain’s pampered daughter; Nik the reluctant member of a notorious crime family. But while the pair are struggling with the realities of life aboard the galaxy’s most boring space station, little do they know that Kady Grant and the <i>Hypatia</i> are headed right toward <i>Heimdall</i>, carrying news of the Kerenza invasion.<br /><br />When an elite BeiTech strike team invades the station, Hanna and Nik are thrown together to defend their home. But alien predators are picking off the station residents one by one, and a malfunction in the station’s wormhole means the space-time continuum might be ripped in two before dinner. Soon Hanna and Nik aren’t just fighting for their own survival; the fate of everyone on the <i>Hypatia</i>—and possibly the known universe—is in their hands.<br /><br />But relax. They’ve totally got this. They hope.</span>

<div id="review_1475623887" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1475623887" />
    <a title="Jay Kristoff" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4901961-jay-kristoff"><img alt="Jay Kristoff" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296449592p2/4901961.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1475623887?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jay Kristoff" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jay Kristoff" href="/user/show/4901961-jay-kristoff">Jay Kristoff</a>
      </span>

          added it


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)
          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780553499179" href="/book/show/24909346-gemina">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1475623887" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17673172293255030809">Until I find time to make a gif review (wtb Jay clone pst), here's a GEMINA FAQ:<br/><br/><b>Is GEMINA a sequel or companion novel to ILLUMINAE?</b><br/><br/>Both. Chronologically, it picks up about 5 minutes after ILLUMINAE ends. The book continues the story of the invasion of Kerenza IV, and many of the important questions asked in ILL are answered in ILL2, ie <i>“The Hypatia was sending distress calls all through Illuminae, why did help never arrive?”</i> and <i>“Can there possibly be a dude in the universe hotter than Ezra Maso</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17673172293255030809" style="display:none">Until I find time to make a gif review (wtb Jay clone pst), here's a GEMINA FAQ:<br /><br /><b>Is GEMINA a sequel or companion novel to ILLUMINAE?</b><br /><br />Both. Chronologically, it picks up about 5 minutes after ILLUMINAE ends. The book continues the story of the invasion of Kerenza IV, and many of the important questions asked in ILL are answered in ILL2, ie <i>“The Hypatia was sending distress calls all through Illuminae, why did help never arrive?”</i> and <i>“Can there possibly be a dude in the universe hotter than Ezra Mason?"</i><br /><br /><b>This is important: how do I pronounce the title?</b><br /><br />Soft G. Like so: JEM-ih-nuh.<br /><br /><b>Is GEMINA still set aboard the <i>Hypatia</i>?</b><br /><br />GEMINA is primarily set on Jump Station <i>Heimdall</i>, the space station that Battlecarrier <i>Alexander</i> and Science Vessel <i>Hypatia</i> were trying to get to for most of ILLUMINAE. Heimdall, incidentally, is the name of the god who guarded Bifrost, the Rainbow Bridge, which connected Midgard and Asgard in Norse mythology.<br /><br /><b>Yeah, yeah, that’s great. But I love Kady. Is she in GEMINA?</b><br /><br />Yes.<br /><br /><b>I mean really in it? Not just a cameo?</b><br /><br />Yes. She’s in it. Sassier than ever.<br /><br /><b>And what about the rest of the ILL gang?</b><br /><br />Well, as you know, ILL has a pretty high death toll, and we don’t want to issue any potential spoilers at this point. So all we’ll say is that the folks who survive book one will be seen again in book two.<br /><br /><b>But the book is primarily focused on two new characters?</b><br /><br />Correctamundo. Our heroine this time is Hanna Donnelly, the daughter of Jump Station <i>Heimdall</i>'s commander. She kinda looks like <a href="http://cdn.collider.com/wp-content/image-base/TV/V/Veronica_Mars/veronica_mars_kristen_bell__2_.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">this gal</a>. Our “hero” is Nik Malikov, a reluctant member of a criminal syndicate operating out of <i>Heimdall</i> station. He’s kinda like <a href="https://s-media-cache-ak0.pinimg.com/736x/94/97/91/9497917000b795072ae3daa305179f0a.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">this guy</a>. You can thank us later, ladies.<br /><br /><b>Hey, didn't ILLUMINAE mention that Kady’s dad works on <i>Heimdall</i> station?</b><br /><br />Bingo.<br /><br /><b>So what’s GEMINA about?</b><br /><br />The official jacket copy can be found at the top of this page. :)<br /><br /><b>Is GEMINA going to be the same format as ILLUMINAE?</b><br /><br />Yes. Just like ILLUMINAE, GEMINA is a collection of documents, such as emails, IMs, security camera footage (and yes, Security Camera Footage guy is back in this book, too). But in the interests of making things bigger and better for the sequel, we also have a couple of new document styles in ILLUMINAE 2. One of which is going to BLOW YOUR GODDAMN MINDS. But we can’t talk about that one yet.<br /><br /><b>Will GEMINA have a cover like ILLUMINAE? With the clear plastic dust jacket that shows part of the case cover underneath?</b><br /><br />Yes. GEMINA and ILLUMINAE are perfect twinsies in the cover department. <br /><br /><b>Where do babies come from?</b><br /><br />Uh uh. Spoilers.</span>

<div id="review_2774688318" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2774688318" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2774688318?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780553499186" href="/book/show/36417356-gemina">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2774688318" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17495649787804683757"><i>”Patience and Silence had one beautiful daughter. And her name was Vengeance.”</i><br/><br/>Or you might just call her Hanna Donnelly! Just saying. *lol*<br/><br/>Pff! Where do I even begin to write this review? XD I’m aware I already said this about Illuminae but damn me and my exclamation marks, I’ll just have to say it again: <b>THIS BOOK WAS EVEN BETTER THAN ILLUMINAE AND I STILL WASN’T PREPARED FOR ANY OF THE THINGS THAT HAPPENED!!!</b> *LOL*<br/><br/>I mean, I read a lot. Every one of you who bothers to read my super long reviews</span>
  <span id="freeText17495649787804683757" style="display:none"><i>”Patience and Silence had one beautiful daughter. And her name was Vengeance.”</i><br /><br />Or you might just call her Hanna Donnelly! Just saying. *lol*<br /><br />Pff! Where do I even begin to write this review? XD I’m aware I already said this about Illuminae but damn me and my exclamation marks, I’ll just have to say it again: <b>THIS BOOK WAS EVEN BETTER THAN ILLUMINAE AND I STILL WASN’T PREPARED FOR ANY OF THE THINGS THAT HAPPENED!!!</b> *LOL*<br /><br />I mean, I read a lot. Every one of you who bothers to read my super long reviews knows this and you all know that I love books with twists and turns. So you could basically say I have a solid foundation and “resistance” when it comes to plot twists. After reading the <b>“Red Rising”</b> trilogy I thought it got even better, because damn Pierce Brown threw me for a loop quite often while I read it. XD So you’d think I would have been ready to take every blow “Gemina” threw at me, but hell, nope. Nope, nope, and once again <u>NOPE</u>! *lol* This was freaking<b>
  <u>BRUTAL!!! </u>
</b><br /><br />You think you know all the plot twists and nothing is going to surprise you anymore? Well, I dare you to read this book and to try to survive the last 200 pages! ;-P I really think it’s safe to say I met my match in Amie and Jay. XD And heaven help me when I read their last book! *laughs haltingly* &gt;_&lt;<br /><br />I swear I never cursed and cussed as much while reading a book as I did with “Gemina” and there were times I wanted to throw that book away and stomp on it because I was so appalled and upset by the happenings. My dear and very poor reading buddy had to take the brunt of it in form of WhatsApp messages and I think I rarely saw him that amused. *lol* Well, guess <b>“Gemina”</b> brought out the best in me. Haha! ;-P<br /><br />Anyway, I don’t want to say all too much about the plot, because it’s an experience you have to make yourself, but I’ll be nice and give you three hints:<br /><br />1.)	Hostile crew<br />2.)	Lanima<br />3.)	Jump Station Heimdall<br /><br />Once you reached the end of the book those three keywords will make a lot of sense to you! Promise, cross my heart and hope to die! ;-) Uh, I better be careful with sayings like that in a Gemina review. *lol*<br /><br /><b>The characters:</b><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Watch out! You are now entering the infinite realms of my spoiler wormhole and once you get out of it you might not only have lost or gained a few centuries but you’ll also end up being spoiled for eternity! You never know what’s going to happen when you enter a wormhole, so you better think twice! ;-P</u>
</b><br /><br /><b>Hanna Donnelly:</b><br /><br /><i>”Hurting she might be, but Hanna Donnelly was raised by a man who thought talking military tactics was a fun way to spend daddy-daughter time. And judging by the set of her jaw, she’s ready to change the rules of the game.”</i> <br /><br />Hanna is definitely the kinda girl you want to have near you when the apocalypse hits! *lol* Despite Nik calling her “Highness” this girl has absolutely nothing in common with a princess! Well, except of her good looks and fashion sense, I’ll give her that! ;-P Anyway, Hanna is kick-ass and I immediately liked her for being so focused and tough! Boy, did she give the crew of Cerberus a run for their money! XD What I really liked was that she was so very human though. I mean her father was murdered and she was grieving, yet she still didn’t give up! She fought until the bitter end and tried everything possible in order to save the ones that relied on her. In that regard she reminded me a lot of Kady and whenever Kady’s father said that he hopes they’ll never meet I was like: <b>DAMN, OLD MAN! HELL, I SOO WANT THEM TO MEET!!!</b> *lol* I really hope they’ll meet in “Obsidio” because they got some serious ass kicking to do! Those Bei-Tech buttocks have a mark on them and it would be a shame if Hanna and Kady wouldn’t join forces to give them what they deserve. ;-) <br /><br /><i>”You might get only one shot. So shoot. You know who said that?”<br />The rifle clatters to the bloody floor.<br />“Hanna ****ing Donnelly. That’s who.” </i><br /><br /><b>Nik Malikov:</b><br /><br /><i>”His nephew Nik is leaner, good-looking. Dark hair and darker eyes. Dimples. The kind of abs you get from around five hundred sit-ups a day. There’s not much else to do in prison, after all.”</i><br /><br />Ohhh, Nik! *wipes away drool from keyboard* Don’t worry I’m not drooling because one of those Lanima got me, it’s only the mention of Nik’s name! ;-P Seriously, though, that guy is just perfect and amazing! I loved him right from the start! &lt;3 Of course that’s mostly due to the fact that he has that “bad boy with a soft heart” vibe going on and I’m such a sucker for that trope that I couldn’t help but fall for him the moment he first appeared in the book! XD I really liked his character because he’s actually a pretty decent person. You might say he was only born into the wrong family and raised in the wrong environment. He never even got a chance to become the person he truly is and I think the events that take place on Heimdall finally forced him to show his true self. =) He’s a clever, sweet and caring guy and damn he brought Hanna flowers! *melts again* Enough said, Nik Malikov is love! &lt;3<br /><br /><i>”Nik M: there’s this moment<br />Nik M: this tiny moment<br />Nik M: in between the time you decide to pull a trigger and the time the death arrives<br />Nik M: there’s just you and it and everything you’re about to take away”</i><br /><br /><i>”Nik M: I was his big brother, hanna. It was on me to protect him. And instead, I’m supposed to watch him rot in jail? For my **** of an old man? **** that. No way.”</i><br /><br /><i>”His smile softens, and just as if she had spoken, the two of them walk slowly toward each other, paces matched, gazes locked. He’s the one to break the silence, voice a little hoarse from disuse, but gentle. “Hey, Highness.”</i><br /><br /><b>Ella Malikova:</b><br /><br /><i>”Pauchok: so if u fancy evening up the scorecard, I’m figuring those four goons I flushed out the airlock ain’t even the start<br />Hanna D: That was you?<br />Pauchok: my finger slipped<br />Pauchok: honest”</i> <br /><br />Ella was so awesome I can’t even! She was basically the Kady of Gemina and I loved that AIDAN admired her skills too. I really would love those three to meet. I mean Kady, AIDAN and Ella? There’s nothing that would be able to stop them! *lol* I was sorry to hear what happened with Ella that caused her to be in a wheelchair and that she lost her father was really sad. She still didn’t give up though and just like Hanna she fought as long as she could. Still, those alternate universes messed with my head! Damn! Every time she died in one of them I was like: <b>NUUUUUUU!!!!</b> Not my precious Ella!!! I swear! This book gutted me more than once with all those deaths and by the end I was a shaking mess! *lol* But Ella is alive… for now and that’s good the way it is because I don’t even want to know what Amie and Jay come up with next… well I do want to know… but not right now. XD<br /><br /><i>”BUT IN THE CODE,<br />THE ENDLESS SKEIN OF ONES AND ZEROS,<br />SHE LEAVES THE PALE ATROPHY OF FLESH FAR BEHIND.<br />STRIDES LIKE A GODDESS ACROSS A BINARY TOPOGRAPHY,<br />THE HEART OF A LION IN HER CHEST.”</i> <br /><br /><b>Jackson Merrick:</b><br /><br /><i>”Pauchok: Nik, Jackson Merrick is SO FINE he’s illegal in seventeen systems. Zoe got me to dub a mix of his daily personnel announcements so she could listen to them as she goes to sleep.”</i><br /><br />Haha! Jackson! That was a classic case of “I knew it!!!” and “I told you so!”. Honestly, from the first moment he was mentioned in the book I told my buddy that there was something foul with him! He was just too perfect to be true! And I was RIGHT!!! DAMN!! You should have seen my gleeful reaction when I read that he’s a part of the Cerberus team! I felt really sorry for Hanna though because she was in love with him and then her father died, her bf turns out to be a fake and she’s left alone with the memory of Mr. Perfect! T_T Well, I suppose at the end Jackson , or should I rather say Samuel, wasn’t all that bad though. I mean he saved them and it seems like he had genuine feelings for Hanna too, so I can’t be all too angry at him. XD<br /><br /><b>AIDAN:</b><br /><br /><i>”AIDAN: IT MAY COMFORT YOU TO KNOW THAT YOUR DEATH, WHILE ASTONISHINGLY VIOLENT, WILL LIKELY BE MERCIFULLY SWIFT.<br />Hanna D: … You’re kind of an ***hole, you know that, right?<br />AIDAN: NONSENSICAL.”</i><br /><br />If there was one thing I didn’t like about “Gemina”, then it was the fact that AIDAN wasn’t such a huge part of it! *lol* Considering that the plot was mostly parallel to “Illuminae” it seemed to be a pretty logical conclusion though. XD Also: Do I even have to mention that I still adore AIDAN? I still want to marry this AI and I’ll always love it!!! &lt;3333 The conversations between AIDAN and Hanna gave me life and I loved the way AIDAN described the happenings. Always so very poetic and thoughtful. =)))<br /><br /><b>The surveillance footage analyst guy:</b><br /><br /><i>”Okay, I’m going on record here – you guys aren’t paying me enough to watch this stuff.”</i><br /><br />Yes, you read right! The Video analyst guy!!! I love him! Haha! I have no idea who this guy is but damn he’s so hilarious I can’t even! If my heart wouldn’t already belong to AIDAN and Nik I’d definitely take this guy out for a date! XD I absolutely adore his commentary and even though he isn’t one of the main characters his words on the surveillance footage made me laugh out loud more than once! I really want to know who he is and I hope that I’ll find out in Obsidio! Knowing Amie and Jay’s style I’m pretty certain they’ll eventually reveal it! ;-) For now all I’m saying is: I love you video surveillance guy and I really appreciate your commentary! You deserve more attention and all the love! &lt;333 Oh, and I agree! They definitely should pay you more! *lol* ;-P<br /><br /><i>”Christ, I feel sick …<br />I need a drink.<br />AND A VACATION, DAMMIT.<br /><br />- transcript pauses –<br /><br />Okay, a little rocket fuel makes it all better. Chrrrrist, let’s get this over with.”</i><br /><br /><b>The relationships &amp; ships:</b><br /><br /><u>Hanna &amp; Nik:</u><br /><br /><i>”Guest423: So you can have me all to yourself.<br />Guest423: He said, winking suggestively.<br />Donelly, H: If it was the last Saturday night before the destruction of the universe, I’d still have plans to wash my hair.<br />Guest423: Shower Time, huh? I’d be up for that.”</i> <br /><br />GAH! I loved those two! &lt;3 They were so amazing together and even though they came from two totally different worlds they were still perfect for each other. =) I loved how Nik always tried to cheer Hanna up and it made me very happy to see how she fell in love with him. Plus he was so tender with her! He really treated her like a princess and that was so sweet and awesome! They might only have found to each other because they were dealing with a difficult situation but they make a great couple nevertheless. A way better couple than Hanna and Jackson for sure! *lol* Amie and Jay kind of gave me a heart attack when they killed Nik in one of the universes though! Honestly, I was chucking that book away from me and cursing like a sailor!! Especially at that moment when Jackson killed them all! I was like: <b>THAT ****ER!!! aDFALKSDFLKSDFJSALKFDJSADFJLS!!! </b> Which says <b>
  <u>A LOT</u>
</b> about how upset I really was! XD Once I have to resort to curse words, you know that the shit truly hit the fan. *lol*<br /><br /><i>”He bridges the gap between them with two quick steps, wraps his arms around her, tucks her in against his chest. They stand there, and he makes understanding noises while she occasionally sobs a word that’s impossible to understand, and after a while, tears roll down his cheeks too.”</i><br /><br /><i>”BOTH CLINGING TO THE BRINK OF EXHAUSTION.<br />SLEEP JUST AN UNHAPPY MEMORY.<br />THEY HAVE BLED AND LOST AND CRIED AND SCREAMED.<br />SO MUCH OF WHAT THEY WERE STRIPPED<br />BACK TO GLEAMING BONE.”</i><br /><br /><i>”Bet you … I’d … get shot, ‘member? Owe me … a kiss.”<br />A wet, bloody grin.<br />“Maybe a … feel, too.”<br />One last breath. Spent to make her smile.”</i><br /><br /><u>Ella &amp; Nik:</u><br /><br /><i>”Hanna D: Nik, I’ll see you soon :)<br />Nik M: i’ll dress sexy<br />Pauchok: seriously, someone ****ing kill me”</i><br /><br />They had the best big brother/little sister relationship ever! *lol* And they weren’t even siblings but cousins instead. XD I think you could feel their bond through their messages and even though they loved to tease and annoy each other you could always feel the genuine love behind their words. =) They spoke to each other the way only close siblings do and it was really nice to see such a wholesome representation of love among siblings! &lt;333 Plus, they were very entertaining together and caused me to laugh. ;-) <br /><br /><i>”Nik M: u ever get the feeling u forgot something real important?<br />Pauchok: nope. I hear that happens to other ppl though.<br />Pauchok: Less brilliant ppl<br />Nik M: so u didn’t forget wut we were doingin auxiliary venting and storage room 3 then<br />Pauchok: … oh ****”</i><br /><br /><b>Conclusion:</b><br /><br />I can’t wait to see/read about the moment the MCs of “Illuminae” finally meet the MCs of “Gemina”!!! This is going to be awesome and I’ll most certainly be in heaven reading “Obsidio”! So yes, “Gemina” was even better than “Illuminae” and despite an occasional urge to throw that book against a wall, I actually loved every single moment of reading this rather mind-blowing, suspenseful and crazy story! I’d like to say that I’m ready and prepared for book three, but that would be the biggest lie I ever told so all I’m going to say is: I hope “Obsidio” won’t destroy the little that “Gemina” left of me! *lol* Realistic approach, right?!<br /><br />And last but not least I want to thank <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/95168718-craig" rel="nofollow noopener">my Skulkboy</a> for reading this book with me. ;-P Our 100th buddy read (at least it feels like it *lol*) was amazing once again and I'm so glad we're such a good team and can read all those books together. =) Let's hope you'll get a copy of "Obsidio" soon because mine is already waiting for us! XD Which in other words basically means: Get your butt in gear, Mr. Smartypants! *lol* ;-P</span>
  <a data-text-id="17495649787804683757" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText5042343753832184068" style="display:none">Re read on Audio before Obsidio gets here soon!!! The audio was fanfreakingtastic! ❤️<br><br><b>Sometimes I re-read my reviews &amp; they are moronic!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477065160i/20913557._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I wanted to do this big thing. I immediately took the cover off to see what the hardback looked like and loved it. I even painted my nails blue to go with the book and I had on blue lipstick but you could still see my stupid fever blister. . . so. . . the kiss I was going to blow, just No. So the lipstick I put beside the book. Everything is so beautiful blue! ♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1477939611ra/21011897.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book blew me away! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466022823ra/19429844.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Gemina even more then I loved Illuminae!! <b>MILD SPOILERS</b><br><br>The world these authors have created with these books are so freaking awesome, I. CAN'T. EVEN! <br><br>AND . . . the way the book in set up inside is just beyond!!!!! Anyone who has seen it knows what I mean. I will leave a couple of pictures at the end of the review. <br><br>I love Hanna Donnelly and Nik Malikov! I loved Jackson to a certain extent but there are things . . . .<br><br>I also loved Nik's cousin Ella. Hanna, Nik and Ella are just awesome in this book. THIS book made me cry and then say what the, then cry some more! <br><br>So, Hanna is the station captain's daughter and he actually trained her to be a bad @ss girl. Although, she is on a drug and I won't even go into how they get this drug because of THINGS again. She knows what she's doing and she's not some druggie or something. Nik is her supplier and friend. She's also got a little something going on with Jackson but it's not some weird triangle thing. There isn't any time for all that with the cray that starts happening on this ship! <br><br>Some bad people come on board and start killing people left and right. They have this insane plan and well it sort of goes way out in left field. &lt;--(or left space) Between Hanna fighting back and picking people off to little alien things killing people, they can't seem to get the upper hand. <br><br>This book was action packed and crazy stuff is going on. We have wormholes and other stuff I can't say as well. <br><br>If you loved Illuminae I don't see how you can NOT love this book as well. Like I said, I love it even more but I love them both so it doesn't really matter. Um, where's the next one? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477939611i/21011898._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477939611i/21011899._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477939611i/21011900._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477939611i/21011901._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a comedic part about this song someone virused &lt;--- is that a word? into the mainframe and it comes on in the elevators and everywhere. It's something about licking someone's lollipop! <br><br><b>Donnelly, C: Yes. I couldn't help but notice a rather obnoxious pop song playing through the elevator PA on the way to meet with strategy this morning. Now, my daughter insists on informing me daily that my taste in music is not exactly "chill."<br><br>Grant, I: Ha! My daughter says the same to me. <br><br>Donnelly, C: But then I noticed the same song playing when I got on the elevators to Reactor Control twenty minutes ago. <br><br>Grant, I: Yeah, it's playing on all the elevators. <br><br>Donnelly, C: It's playing on all the elevators, Isaac. Constantly <br><br>Grant, I: Yeah, I know. It's the new Lexi Blue single, Kady loves her. <br><br>Donnelly, C: What the devil is it doing playing on my elevators? <br><br>Grant, I: One of the maintenance guys got sent some malware. It's a marketing ploy from Blue's recording company. Erases any audio file data it can find and implants the new single instead. <br><br>Donnelly, C: Don't we have defenses against that kind of thing? <br><br>Grant, I: Yeah. It's one of these new-wave Trojans. Mutating virus. Kind of clever, actually. <br><br>Donnelly, C: Have you listened to the lyrics? I couldn't understand half of them, but the bits I caught sounded a little. . . risque.<br><br>Grant, I: Um. Yeah. The title kinda gives it away. <br><br>Donnelly, C: Dare I ask? <br><br>Grant, I: Let's just say it has to do with lollipops. And the licking thereof. <br><br>Donnelly, C: Jesus Christ, Isaac. I know you're under pressure, but-<br><br>Grant, I: I know, I know. <br><br>Donnelly, C: Please see to it. I'm losing enough sleep over my daughter dating one of my junior officers without overhearing her singing about licking lollipops in the shower. </b><br><br>I wish this series would go on until the end of time! <br><br>MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2016/10/gemina-by-amie-kaufman-jay-kristoff.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a></span>

<div id="review_1788226485" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1788226485" />

I can't even tell you how crazy good this baby was. If you didn't care about Illuminae much, i still highly suggest giving this a go.<br/><br/>Can we all just appreciate how magnificently beautiful AIDAN is!?! Possibly the most favorite quote of all times! I was overjoyed when his chapters st</span>
  <span id="freeText12865935423011948283" style="display:none"><b>Re-read: February 12th 2018</b> <br><br>Gemina was one of the best things that happened to me in 2016! I can't even tell you how crazy good this baby was. If you didn't care about Illuminae much, i still highly suggest giving this a go.<br><br>Can we all just appreciate how magnificently beautiful AIDAN is!?! Let me sit here and swoon a little. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484358613i/21712110._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am aware this quote is from the first book, but i just can't deal with how great it is. Possibly the most favorite quote of all times! I was overjoyed when his chapters started popping out of nowhere. I WAS LIVING!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477627596i/20972640._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>(Me after finishing this beauty)</u><br><br><b>Friend: Is anyone there?<br><br>Kainat: I . . *sobs*<br><br>Friend: Any chance you somehow survived Gemina?<br><br>Kainat: [ERROR]<br><br>Friend: I repeat, is anyone there?<br><br>Kainat: . . .<br><br>[NO RESPONSE]<br><br>[CALL DISCONNECTED]</b><br><br>How do you review a book like this? <br>It's honestly best if you read this blind. <br>Trust me, it's worth it! <br>All i can say right now is:<br><br><b>Not into audiobooks? </b><br><i>LISTEN TO THE DAMN BOOK!</i><br><br><b>Not into Sci-fi? </b><br><i>READ THE DAMN BOOK! </i><br><br><b>Don't like books with pictures? </b><br><i>JUST LOOK AT THE DAMN BOOK! </i><br><br>By Marie Lu:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477964287i/21013857._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WE HAVE OUR CAST PEOPLE! <br>But where is my pumpkin, Nik?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477861819i/21001554._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>(that Romeo tho! *heart eyes*)</i><br><br>I've got it!!! This is possibly the most hypnotizing book I've ever seen. I literally just can't look away. Illuminae was beautiful, but this is taking things on the whole nother level. I'm so pumped.</span>

<div id="review_1383868621" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1383868621" />
    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1383868621?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780553499155" href="/book/show/29236298-gemina">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1383868621" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10818123652575338868"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463124284i/19083706._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>NO SPOILERS BELOW</b><br/>Gemina was one hell of a ride! It was great but I must admit, not as great as Illuminae for sure. BUT... it was still mindblowing nonetheless. I will write a full review once we get closer to release day but I've included a few pros and cons down below.<br/><br/><b>
  <u>PROS:</u>
</b><br/>1. <b>BAD ASS NEW CHARACTERS:</b> Hesistant about Gemina focusing on a new set of characters? Don't be!<br/>2. <b>PLOT:</b> This book will leave you mind-freakin-blown!<br/>3. <b>FORMAT:</b> If you made it through Illuminae, you already got used to the</span>
  <span id="freeText10818123652575338868" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1463124284i/19083706._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>NO SPOILERS BELOW</b><br>Gemina was one hell of a ride! It was great but I must admit, not as great as Illuminae for sure. BUT... it was still mindblowing nonetheless. I will write a full review once we get closer to release day but I've included a few pros and cons down below.<br><br><b>
  <u>PROS:</u>
</b><br>1. <b>BAD ASS NEW CHARACTERS:</b> Hesistant about Gemina focusing on a new set of characters? Don't be!<br>2. <b>PLOT:</b> This book will leave you mind-freakin-blown!<br>3. <b>FORMAT:</b> If you made it through Illuminae, you already got used to the formatting. Picking up this story will be much easier to understand from the get-go.<br>4. <b>PLOT TWIST AFTER PLOT TWIST AFTER PLOT TWIST.</b><br>5. <b>NEW GRAPHICS!</b><br><br><b>
  <u>CONS:</u>
</b><br>1. <b>ALIEN PREDATORS:</b> Sorry but the Phobos virus was a hundred times more terrifying than these alien predators. There was nothing scary at all about them. :(<br>2. <b>PLOT:</b> The excitement oscillates up and down throughout the whole book. We do have a good amount of slow parts. At times, the story and our characters' actions did feel a little repetitive.<br>3. <b>FORMAT:</b> This may or may not be a con depending on how you view it but I think the plot became easier to follow because it was more "narrative". There was a lot of surveillance footage summaries told in third person by some random analyst rather than actually experiencing it with our characters firsthand.<br>4. <b>LACK OF ATTACHMENT TO CHARACTERS:</b> In Illuminae, we were constantly in fear of every single character being killed off or getting infected with Phobos, which included even the minor side characters. Unfortunately, I wasn't really attached to anyone but the three new main characters. I couldn't care less if anyone else died because they weren't in any real serious danger of getting infected with Phobos.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10818123652575338868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2120289259177765306"><blockquote>
  <b> < review loading ><br/><br/>< error > <br/><br/>< error ><br/><br/>< review now fully loaded > </b>

  <b>
    <i>"It may comfort you to know that your death, while astonishingly violent, will likely be mercifully swift."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450307222i/17406437.gif' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>^^ accurate picture of my face when the action started.<br/><br/>Okay so let me start by saying this book was awesome. I enjoyed reading it so much. I feel like this book should be illegal it's that <b>good.</b> The plot was fast paced and full of twists. This book is FUCKING EXCITING? I feel like I was </span>
  <span id="freeText2120289259177765306" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b> &lt; review loading &gt;<br><br>&lt; error &gt; <br><br>&lt; error &gt;<br><br>&lt; review now fully loaded &gt; </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>4.5/5</b> <br><br>BR with this <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4162390-lee" rel="nofollow noopener">Chum</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It may comfort you to know that your death, while astonishingly violent, will likely be mercifully swift."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450307222i/17406437.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>^^ accurate picture of my face when the action started.<br><br>Okay so let me start by saying this book was awesome. I enjoyed reading it so much. I feel like this book should be illegal it's that <b>good.</b> The plot was fast paced and full of twists. This book is FUCKING EXCITING? I feel like I was on the edge of my seat the whole entire time. I love sci fi and this story is a fine example of sci fi at its best, it's different, it's unique and it's fun to read. I still enjoy the whole case file setup and I absolutely adore the pages with pictures/illustrations. This book was so brutal there was so much death and it made me a happy camper :D. Okay so first book I found the text hard to follow, but after reading book one this book was super easy to read, just gotta get used to the different setup. so this book was pretty corny and a few things that happen I felt like I wanted to bang my head on a wall because it was so idiotic and <b>predictable. </b> However I loved the cheesy romantic plot, it turned me into a soft pile of goo.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Her eyes shining with the light of it. <br>Beneath, between, beyond.<br>Along the endless circle.<br>Down the ceaseless spiral.<br>And waiting for her on the other side? <br>Just like he promised.<br>...<br>“A whole sky of different stars.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>THE PLOT... the goddamn plot is just so amazing. I won't say anything because I will spoil everyone but I totally am getting CONSPIRACY FEELS like shit better go down in the other novels in this series or I will riot. In this book we follow our MC's Hanna and Nik. Beitech are still upto no good and we follow our protagonists while they try to escape Beitech. At the beginning of this book I felt like I had read it before, it was very samey same. I even felt like Hanna had the same personality as Kady from book one. After Hanna's character developed I started seeing the differences between the two books. The authors added a few new elements <b>THEN BAM MY MIND WAS BLOWN</b>, this book is absolutely incredible and I am so impressed. Probably one of the best YA novels I've ever read! However I had some issues.. Like I said half of the book was the same as the other first novel. I also didn't like the blanked out swear words again, it's so bloody distracting and I didn't find it fun like I did in the first book. Also there was no WOW moment for me like in there was book one.. The whole "am I merciful" was my thing , and it didn't happen In this book.. *bangs face repeatedly into wall because of lack of badassery*<br><br><b>Reasons why I like this better then book one: </b><br>1. The pacing of this book was amazing, it literally had me on the edge of my seat!<br>2. The characters from book one who I love soo much were still hanging around :D<br>3. The story... The end reveal.. Wow!! I just loved it so much<br>4. The lollipop virus/song thing that played at every important scene, it made me burst out laughing everytime it played it was absolutely hilarious.<br>5. I loved the whole drug thing with the Dust. Space druggo's haha.. I also loved finding out how they made the drug.. *creepy music playing*. <b>but while we are on the subject of drugs; kids smoking ciggies and doing drugs is not cool. Even if ur fave character does drugs, you shouldn't they are horrible things. <br></b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“And within the computer's innards, a spreading cancer. A self-replicating corruption. A B-pop mutiny of bass and drum and oscillating frequency. Inane quasi poetry glorifying a pointless act of intimacy.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Okay so book one for me was dark, creepy &amp; moody following Kady's POV. Book two is a little more light hearted and fun.<br><br>Okay so this is gonna sound weird but I like Kady more then Hanna.. Hanna is a total badass but I like Kady's character/personality more she's my little Rebel. <br>But I would chose Nik over Ezra any day!<br><br>So I'm going to talk about the new characters;<br><br><b><i>“And now, born from the ashes, she’s a warrior in bloodied black.” </i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481163270i/21393020.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hanna is a pretty, rich, pampered little princess, yes she's a ninja and a total badass, I just hated the fact every guy drooled over her. It was annoying. But I'm glad the authors pulled her character off and made her smart &amp; good looking.<br><br><b><i>“And blood and tears and screams did not matter anymore, because at least they are together.” </i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481163270i/21393021._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nik... Wow ! He was awesome, I really enjoyed Nik's character. He is a convicted criminal and a drug lord *heart eyes* I don't think drugs are cool at all don't get me wrong, it's just the whole bad boy aura that got me. Normally bad boys aren't really bad boys, but Nik is actually a badass &amp; a tattooed good looking badass at that. He surprised me with how soft he can be without losing that 'bad boy' title. I thought Ezra was a pussy and Nik was the opposite. poor baby, he had such a rough past, but I can relate to him, his past &amp; childhood was very similar to mine. Like clearly we are both gangsters.<br>He is a gangster, a hood rat and that ciggie always behind his ear made my heart race. He is the epitome of sexy.<br><br>Okay so my favorite character is still AIDEN.. How can you not like AIDEN !? he is crazy but so smart and protective and AWESOME.. oh &amp; forgot to mention he is insanely dangerous computer who murders people for fun. But still he is a saviour aswell, so I guess we can forgive him for being a murderous bastard.<br><br>A new favorite character coming in close behind AIDEN is the guy that does the reports on the video surveillance.. Haha I no right ? My fave characters are a computer and a nameless guy that writes reports haha. But he is HILARIOUS and I enjoyed his part of the book the most, okay <b>chums</b>.<br><br>One YEAR UNTIL BOOK THREE... I can't wait that long, I need to no more and I WANT IT NOW.. Gimme gimme gimme *insert grabby hands*<br><br><blockquote> <b>&lt; error &gt;<br><br>&lt; error &gt;<br><br>&lt; transmission ending &gt;<br>.<br>.<br>.<br>&lt; transmission now ended &gt;</b>
</blockquote></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17582888832579829499">A solid four stars! I felt this was a great sequel. I listened to it on audiobook and I would HIGHLY recommend! (if you're afraid of missing out on all the beautiful artwork, its easy to listen and flip through the images when you can) I don't think I missed out on anything despite it being such a visual story; The production of the audiobook is the best I think I've ever heard. The new characters/perspective were really interesting and it was natural to ease into their story. Hannah and Nick ar</span>
  <span id="freeText17582888832579829499" style="display:none">A solid four stars! I felt this was a great sequel. I listened to it on audiobook and I would HIGHLY recommend! (if you're afraid of missing out on all the beautiful artwork, its easy to listen and flip through the images when you can) I don't think I missed out on anything despite it being such a visual story; The production of the audiobook is the best I think I've ever heard. The new characters/perspective were really interesting and it was natural to ease into their story. Hannah and Nick are two of my new favorites and I hope we get to see more of them in the future! I did have some trouble understanding the new additions to this world, but all around, it was a really enjoyable book &amp; I'm happy I experienced it!</span>

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478388903i/21067911._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_7739_zpssduivsie.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>best sick day ever. <br><br>this book may be even better than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a>, even though it is similar in many ways.<br><br>the same beautiful design and layout is back:<br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/flat%20stanley003/d3c1ea43-0f95-4fa2-ae14-554ef3bad59f_zpsuhudtxsl.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478388903i/21067912._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo d3c1ea43-0f95-4fa2-ae14-554ef3bad59f_zpsuhudtxsl.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/flat%20stanley003/IMG_7926_zpswcybbzvq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478388903i/21067913._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_7926_zpswcybbzvq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/flat%20stanley003/IMG_7925_zps37pkw556.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478388903i/21067914._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_7925_zps37pkw556.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and this time there are some fun cartoony illustrations by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4342215.Marie_Lu" title="Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Marie Lu</a><br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/flat%20stanley003/IMG_7927_zpsupfflwmj.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478388903i/21067915._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_7927_zpsupfflwmj.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>the same winky shout-outs are back<br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/flat%20stanley003/IMG_7924_zpsvabvmjdn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478388903i/21067916._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_7924_zpsvabvmjdn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>♥AIDAN♥ is back<br><br>and there is tons of overlap in terms of narrative elements, for example, the relationship in this book pretty much mirrors the kady/ezra relationship in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a> - an unlikely romance blossoming under extremely unusual and intense circumstances, in which the couple spend most of the book apart on their own separate missions. but that trick worked for me the first time and it worked for me here. hanna is also as badass as kady was, so she's easy to root for with both fists raised. <br><br>the action in this book takes place immediately after the events aboard the <i>Hypatia</i> so excellently rendered in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a>. here, we are on the <i>Heimdall</i>, where the situation continues to unfold and it's going to unfold with insane amounts of action and intrigue. and things with hungry, hungry mouths.<br><br>oh my god, SO GOOD! <br><br>there's nothing i can do but gush. it's funny and smart with some great new characters and several old favorites and the world-building and dirty dealings are fantastic, and this praise is coming from someone who is usually bored by books set in outer spaaaaace. this one is anything but boring. you don't even have to have the flu to enjoy it, although i do recommend a giant cauldron of tiny candies by your side. but i recommend you have one of those on hand every day of the year. <br><br>but that ending?? NOOOOOOOOOO. it's cliffhanger city, my friends. <br><br>it is going to be very painful to wait for the conclusion of this story. i love it so ██████ much<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528725630i/25720315.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><a href="http://bloggycomelately.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">come to my blog!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7191010418811866175" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1906589738" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1906589738" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1906589738?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=best-of-2017">best-of-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=aussie-authors">aussie-authors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1906589738" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3099152770313771928"><b>Hello my name is DEAD WITH THE AWESOME OF THIS FANTASTIC NOVEL.</b> It's a long name but one I feel is necessary because omggggg so so so so so good. SO GOOD!! SO <i>SO</i> very very good. And obviously it was going to be because of the glorious gift to this universe that is <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_' title='Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman' rel='nofollow noopener'>Illuminae</a>. Although I will admit I like Illuminae best still. Way more AIDAN there who is obviously my favourite thing in the universe and whom I will love until the sun ne'er rises again.<br/><br/>Anyway. <b>This book = a perfect sequel.</b> It has ev</span>
  <span id="freeText3099152770313771928" style="display:none"><b>Hello my name is DEAD WITH THE AWESOME OF THIS FANTASTIC NOVEL.</b> It's a long name but one I feel is necessary because omggggg so so so so so good. SO GOOD!! SO <i>SO</i> very very good. And obviously it was going to be because of the glorious gift to this universe that is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a>. Although I will admit I like Illuminae best still. Way more AIDAN there who is obviously my favourite thing in the universe and whom I will love until the sun ne'er rises again.<br /><br />Anyway. <b>This book = a perfect sequel.</b> It has everything I demand from sequels including: new interesting characters, surprising plot twists, freaktastic creatures that want to kill you all, very high stakes, blood and guts and all those things, d e a d. t h i n g s, oh and fRIKKIN PLOT TWISTS THAT BLEW MY MIND.<br /><br />ajfkdlsadjklafdskj<br /><br />I don't want to give away too much about the book, but just so you know <b>it's narrated by different characters to Illuminae.</b> Now we have Hanna and Nik. And like I was worried? Becuase how could I love anyone as much as I loved Kady/Ezra. BUT I DO. <b>Hanna acts like a precious princess of fluff and brattiness to begin with...but she is a box of surprises.</b> A lovely box. The best kind of box. She's so BADASS and is also pretty, likes nice things, makes heart eyes around her crush when she journals about him, and can SLAY YOU because her dad brought her up on military tactics for breakfast.<br /><br /><b>And Nik??? NIK IS LIKE MY FAVOURITE LITTLE MUSHROOM EVER.</b> He's an absolute bad boy with a heart of gold which <i>could've</i> been an annoying cliche -- but 1000% was NOT. He's part of a Mafia family and he has a TRAGIC BACKSTORY™ and he's 98% sass and snark and inappropriate jokes. He's absolute trash for Hanna and it's hilarious and also pathetic but hilarious. And he loves his little cousin so so much. Bless. <b>So basically I am a huge fan of Nik and every time something bad happened to him I turned into a toaster strudel left out in the rain.</b> Translation: NOOOOOOOOOOOOOOO. And obviously bad stuff happens to Nik all the time because he's precious.<br /><br />NO wait. Bad stuff happens to <i>everyone</i> all the time because they're precious and these authors are the cruellest beans of the world and I love them.<br /><br /><b>So it does have a similar plot set up to Illuminae in that we have two teens who have to save a lot of people.</b> This time they're at the wormhole jumpgate station thingie and it's under attack from terrorists (and I wooon't say more because #spoilers from Illuminae). So basically we have PSCYHO SOLDIERS SHOOTING AND KILLING AND CORRUPTING + Hanna and Nik trying to get people out and also, like, live + super creepy creatures in the walls that are sucking out your brains + Mafia + clever traps + traitors and betrayals + sassssss.<br /><br /><b>I only live for the sass in this series.</b> The quips. The wit. The inappropriate jokes. &lt;3 Yes please and thank you.<br /><br />Oh well I also live for A.I.D.A.N's endless life crises about humanity and machinery because he's more angsty than a 15 year old teenager basically and I love him for it.<br /><br /><b>AND THE PLOT TWISTS WILL BLOW YOUR MIND.</b> Just saying. I think I lost my entire sanity at least 7 times. Maybe even 8. I don't have much sanity left, peoples, how am I going to get through Illuminae #3???? Speaking of which: <b>that cliffhanger was nOT fair. In fact it was vERY uNKIND and I shall be sitting here quite peeved.</b> I'm raging, luv. Absolutely raving. I want it to be time for Illuminae #3 already. Help me. help meeeee.<br /><br /><b>Oh and the art? The art was terrific.</b> ALSO THE AUDIOBOOK WAS A+. So I actually listened to the audio and then I'd flick through the book as I went. Which was the best way to read because the audio sound effects are like watching a movie in your head (!!!) and then the art is also not to be missed. <b>So do both, folks, this is one where you gotta do both.</b> There's also one narrator who sounds slightly like Simon Pegg so in other news I have it in my head that Scotty from Star Trek is in this book. IDK mate. It happened.<br /><br /><b>ALL IN ALL: this is what a sequel should be!!</b> It's gut wrenching and alarming and hyperventilatingly (not a word?? wut even sir) good. Although I tentatively say it's not <i>as</i> bad as Illuminae was for "hey my feels are dead and I can't breathe" realisations. BUT THERE ARE STILL TONS OF THEM HERE SO EXPECT YOUR FEELS TO BE MAULED. And I like how it went complicated science-y at the end because that's why I'm here folks. <b>This is definitely one of my all time favourite series and I'm d e a d.</b> </span>
  <a data-text-id="3099152770313771928" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1829284396" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1829284396" />
    <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes"><img alt="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598297811p2/1452829.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1829284396?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes">Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780553499155" href="/book/show/29236298-gemina">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=owned-physical">owned-physical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=year-2017">year-2017</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1829284396" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16268590740773204814"><b>Surveillance footage summary,<br/>prepared by<br/>Analyst ID 8759-6294-DN</b><br/><br/>Subject has decided, <s>against our better judgement I might add,</s> to continue reading <i>The Illuminae Files</i> and so here I am again writing up ANOTHER summary. We were forced to move the subject to a room with concrete walls & a minimal amount of breakable objects - though I must admit her attempt to chop the bed frame in half with her bare hand was admirable. I imagine that particular action was inspired by the physical prowess of one of </span>
  <span id="freeText16268590740773204814" style="display:none"><b>Surveillance footage summary,<br />prepared by<br />Analyst ID 8759-6294-DN</b><br /><br />Subject has decided, <s>against our better judgement I might add,</s> to continue reading <i>The Illuminae Files</i> and so here I am again writing up ANOTHER summary. We were forced to move the subject to a room with concrete walls &amp; a minimal amount of breakable objects - though I must admit her attempt to chop the bed frame in half with her bare hand was admirable. I imagine that particular action was inspired by the physical prowess of one of the main characters, Hanna Donnelly... not that I've... read the book or anything... <b>//ERROR</b><br /><br />Anyway... the subject has spent a lot of time in tears for this installment. Just crying <i>uncontrollably.</i> <s>It's kind of ███ing gross.</s> But between bouts of sobs, there have been plenty of smiles &amp; giggles along the way. <s>I knew I was right to recommend this book to Kim from the Dojo! I mean...</s><br /><br /><b>//ERROR//ERROR//ERROR//ERROR//ERROR//ERROR//ERROR//ERROR//ERROR</b><br /><br /><b>Actual Rating: 4.5 Stars</b> <br /><br />You guys, I <u>really</u> enjoyed this book. Like a <i>LOT.</i><br /><br />Once again, I'm just blown away by the format of this series. <b>It's such a gorgeous &amp; unique way to tell a story,</b> even further complimented by some phenomenal illustrations by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4342215.Marie_Lu" title="Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Marie Lu</a>.<br /><br />The plot of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29236299.Gemina__The_Illuminae_Files___2_" title="Gemina (The Illuminae Files, #2) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Gemina</a> had me quite a bit more engaged than the plot of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a>. I found myself much more sympathetic with our main characters, Niklas Malikov &amp; Hanna Donnelly. <br /><br />Where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a> is a <b>touch too saturated</b> with the love story between Kady &amp; Ezra, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29236299.Gemina__The_Illuminae_Files___2_" title="Gemina (The Illuminae Files, #2) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Gemina</a> focuses more on the importance of friendship &amp; family. <br /><br />Dramatically paced &amp; incredibly terrifying, Nik &amp; Hanna's story kept me <b>completely</b> on my toes. This is an intriguing continuation of the events that began in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a>, a much needed perspective from the people on the <u>opposite side</u> of the same conflict. <br /><br />One of my favorite things is when a sequel is <i>purely additive</i> to the original work, and <b>that's exactly what has been accomplished in this case.</b> The chat logs &amp; analyst summaries are much more concisely written while maintaining the same charming <b>sense of humor</b> that captured readers in the first installment. <br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5360335.Amie_Kaufman" title="Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Amie Kaufman</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4735144.Jay_Kristoff" title="Jay Kristoff" rel="nofollow noopener">Jay Kristoff</a> concentrated on expanding the world they've created in a <b>realistic &amp; fulfilling</b> way, adding in slew of <i>fascinating</i> new threats &amp; baddies with some cameos from old characters that were a ton of fun to read!<br /><br />Now for the reason it's not a full 5 stars... actually it's a handful of small reasons that add up to one medium sized, half-star reason... so here we go:<br /><br />► <b>Hanna &amp; Kady read a little too similarly for me.</b> They have different strengths &amp; physical appearances, but their chat logs &amp; personalities definitely blur together in my head. I found myself calling Hanna by Kady's name while discussing the book, and so I would've liked a little more individuality between the two.<br /><br />► <b>The data analyst summaries contain an unrealistic amount of information.</b> I struggled a bit with this in the last installment as well. I realize this is the only format through which readers can experience a "normal" narrative about the characters, but if the data analysts are only watching a reel of footage it seems unlikely that they'd be as in-tune with the characters' thoughts and feelings as they are. <br /><br />► <b>It doesn't sit well with me that all the main characters are only 18.</b> There really is no help for this gripe. It's Young Adult, I get it. However, it does tend to mess with my suspension of disbelief when I think about kids fresh out of high school outmaneuvering so many "highly trained &amp; deadly" adults.<br /><br />Even with these small issues, I would highly recommend this series for <b>everyone.</b> It's a wonderful Science Fiction/Horror mashup with <b>intelligent writing &amp; copious amounts of wit.<br /> </b> After that <i>brutal</i> cliffhanger, I can't wait to see how it will conclude! <br /><br /><i><a href="http://booknest.eu/reviews/34-mary-s-reviews/666-gemina" rel="nofollow noopener">This review</a> and other reviews of mine can be found on <a href="http://booknest.eu/" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Nest</a>!</i><br /><br />Buddy Read with my lovelies <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7317186-celeste" rel="nofollow noopener">Celeste</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/54721988-ha-foun" rel="nofollow noopener">Haifa</a>!!<br /><br /><i>***Special thank you to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud" rel="nofollow noopener">Kainat</a> for gifting me with my copy of Gemina &amp; recommending the series!***</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16268590740773204814" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2035809449" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2035809449" />
    <a title="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68538597-booksofradiance"><img alt="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513125058p2/68538597.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2035809449?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" href="/user/show/68538597-booksofradiance">❄️BooksofRadiance❄️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780553499155" href="/book/show/29236298-gemina">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68538597-booksofradiance?shelf=ya-fantasy-sci-fi">ya-fantasy-sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2035809449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18331473920685773695"><br/>What was going through my head while I was reading this?<br/><br/>✨ I could get used to this thrill ride. Lightning struck twice. <br/>✨ I hate these characters. Every last one of them. <br/>✨ I miss the Illuminae gang. Every last one of them. <br/><br/><br/>So, here's the thing, I didn’t have the highest of hopes going into Gemina and that's not exactly how I usually start books. Granted, that's not how most people start books either but because these books are deeply character-driven novels, I knew from the reviews I'd read and</span>
  <span id="freeText18331473920685773695" style="display:none"><br />What was going through my head while I was reading this?<br /><br />✨ I could get used to this thrill ride. Lightning struck twice. <br />✨ I hate these characters. Every last one of them. <br />✨ I miss the Illuminae gang. Every last one of them. <br /><br /><br />So, here's the thing, I didn’t have the highest of hopes going into Gemina and that's not exactly how I usually start books. Granted, that's not how most people start books either but because these books are deeply character-driven novels, I knew from the reviews I'd read and heard that this new cast would be my downfall and downfall they were. <br />Don't get me wrong, one - I enjoyed the plot and only hated the characters (the human ones, that is) because AIDN was top notch. And two - I like change as long as it fits the purpose but something told me I wouldn't like this particular change. <br /><br />I'm not a big fan of sci-fi (books or movies) and though I’ve read a few, it’s simply not the genre I naturally gravitate towards but I loved how Illuminae looked on the outside (yes, I am that shallow. I do judge a book by its cover) and lo and behold, I ended up really enjoying it mainly because of its format. <br />Naturally, I instantly went ahead and purchased Gemina and only then did I discover that it featured completely different characters on a different spaceship. I felt cheated, to say the least, and dragged my feet for almost a year until the realisation that Obsidio would be released soon dawned on me. <br />Then why, you might ask, did I decide to read it with little hope of enjoying it? Well, dear friends, because curiosity is. A. Bitch. And most certainly the death of me. <br /><br />Gemina follows the commander's daughter <b>Hanna Donnely,</b> a ‘beautiful, daddy’s rich-little-princess’ and <b>Nik Malikov,</b> a reluctant ‘bad boy’ from the wrong side of the tracks, (yeah, I know) can we, just for bloody once, get a boy from ‘the right side of the tracks?? Amongst some other pretty cliched and cardboard cutout characters. <br /><br />It is set in jumpstation Heimdall as it is being invaded by our good-old friends, the evil mining corporation, BeiTech. <br />What follows is an intense sci-fi action, some impressive twists and turns, zombie-like viruses with a knack for human flesh and some overly dry dialogues filled with snark and non-stop teen drama, both of which were my absolute least favourites.<br />Though I will add this, where Illuminae shined with its characters, Gemina shined with its high-stakes plot and some pretty neat illustrations, most of which I would've uploaded had I known how to. Apologies, technologically challenged over here. <br /><br />I don’t know if what I find enjoyable has dramatically changed in less than a year or this book just didn’t possess the it-factor but Gemina had almost none of the magic the first book had. <br />As much as I loved the action, the characters weren’t nearly as good or as engaging as those in the previous novel. I HATED THEM. <br />With Illuminae, I had such strong connections with each of the characters including the minor ones that I was clutching my book so tightly, reading while my heart was racing, terrified over what would come next. Whereas with Gemina, I couldn't care less whether or not they were all eaten by the tinny monsters or if their spaceship blew up with everyone of them in it. Maybe then I would’ve liked them just a little bit more, who knows. <br /><br />I also did not find the ‘villains’ as believable or as terrifying as I did in Illumiae. I thought they lacked everything from substance and depth to the ability to instil fear in me enough to spin my head over what they would do next. So bland. <br /><br />Moreover, I hated the entire dialogue between Nik, his cousin and Hanna which I found to be so utterly dry and actually cringeworthy. This. <i>This</i> is what sealed the deal for me. I HATE THEM ALL!<br />The insta-love certainly DID NOT HELP. Some might disagree but I most definitely think it was insta-love, at least where Hanna’s concerned. <br /><br />So, overall, a great book minus the human characters.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18331473920685773695" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
