<div id="review_1913447904" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1913447904" />
    <a title="emma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32879029-emma"><img alt="emma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520568130p2/32879029.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1913447904?book_show_action=true">Jul 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="emma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="emma" href="/user/show/32879029-emma">emma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780553499155" href="/book/show/29236298-gemina">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=couldn-t-wait-to-read">couldn-t-wait-to-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=unpopular-opinion">unpopular-opinion</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=eh">eh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32879029-emma?shelf=funny">funny</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1913447904" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6200245459264817325">Ah, good fantasy. (Please read with the exact voice and emotional expression of the Spongebob Squarepants narrator soothingly intoning, <i>Ah, Goo Lagoon.</i> If you do not know this reference, please go educate yourself on the tenets of modern culture, <s>you uncultured swine.</s>) BUT WAS IT ACTUALLY GOOD FANTASY?! Now I regret typing that long Spongebob allusion. But not enough to remove it. It took too long. I cannot waste these amazing pop-culture references.<br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.com/2017/09/08/gemina-review/'>https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.co...</a><br/><br/>I am v</span>
  <span id="freeText6200245459264817325" style="display:none">Ah, good fantasy. (Please read with the exact voice and emotional expression of the Spongebob Squarepants narrator soothingly intoning, <i>Ah, Goo Lagoon.</i> If you do not know this reference, please go educate yourself on the tenets of modern culture, <s>you uncultured swine.</s>) BUT WAS IT ACTUALLY GOOD FANTASY?! Now I regret typing that long Spongebob allusion. But not enough to remove it. It took too long. I cannot waste these amazing pop-culture references.<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.com/2017/09/08/gemina-review/">https://emmareadstoomuch.wordpress.co...</a><br><br>I am very aggravated and confused. I am a heap of conflicting emotions. (Yes, a heap. That is not a pile of sundress and cynicism and sort-of-blonde hair in the corner, as you may have presumed, but rather an overwhelmed Me. Please do not be alarmed, for this is my natural state.)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499876090ra/23277105.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Quick concept of what Gemina is: like, five hundred years in the future. Humans livin’ in space. Lots of tech-y, future-y stuff like black holes and jump stations and complicated maybe-science I don’t understand. We follow Hannah (?), our main character/pretty lil rich girl; Nik, her sexual harasser who is supposedly charming; and Ella, THE LOVE OF MY LIFE. We’ll get into all that.<br><br>Sometimes me and <i>Gemina</i> got along like a sense of humor and the movie The Big Sick (which is to say, very well) but I also had SO MANY PROBLEMS WITH IT.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499876090ra/23277106.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>(The Big Sick, on the other hand, caused me neither emotional trial nor emotional tribulation. Just an all-out fantastic movie. Do I have a bigger crush on Kumail Nanjiani or Emily V. Gordon? Who’s to say.) (Did Emily V. Gordon like my tweet? Yes. I’m cool. I’m fine. I’m casual. What? No, there was no squealing to be heard. That would be ridiculous. Not chill at all.)<br><br>The Big Sick love-rant over. Unless you don’t see it. In which case I will pen a review of The Big Sick, drive to your hometown, take you to a showing of said film with all necessary force, and whisper the review of the movie to you during the quiet parts of this same movie. (And on top of it, you will be the one paying for the tickets. Movie theaters are expensive and I am not made of money.)<br><br>You guys when I started screaming at you about an unrelated movie rather than screaming about this book:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499876090ra/23277107.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay. I’m done. I really am. <s>But go see The Big Sick.</s><br><br>Let’s start with the good stuff, I guess. (About Gemina. You know, the book I’m allegedly reviewing.)<br><br>Time has passed, I am wearing rose colored glasses (and rocking them, obvs) and I’m mostly remembering the good stuff. Good sign for this book! Let’s talk about fun and nice things.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499876090ra/23277108.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>THE GOOD</b><br><br>1. THESE BOOKS ARE JUST SO CLEVER.<br>You really have to hand it to them. Like, my bois (the term “boi” has always been gender neutral to me) Kristoff and Kaufman straight KILLED. IT. in terms of formatting. All those chat logs and sketches (new addition to this book) and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[amazingly creepy and fun death countdown of the bad guys <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Loved it, man. It feels way smoother than the Illuminae formatting. And don’t even get me started on AIDAN, the semi-evolved computer whose nefarious and creepy inner workings are...used to summarize surveillance footage. But we’re veering toward negatives so I’ll move on. Long story short, why do traditionally-formatted books even still exist?!<br><br>2. I HAVE A NEW BFF.<br>I would say “gf,” but she’s fifteen years old and also I’d rather just become her than anything else. Her name is Ella Malikova and she is a hacker. (YOU SHOULD ALL KNOW BY NOW THAT I AM SUCH A SUCKER FOR A HACKER. Is there any better plot than a heist with a hacker character? Baby Driver should’ve had a hacker.) (Also, see Baby Driver too.) Anyway, she is so funny and badass and I love her so much. #GiveEllaMalikovaHerOwnBook2k17<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499876090ra/23277109.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>3. This book be funny<br>There’s some made up slang in here, which I like. (Somehow it makes sense with context clues but also isn’t overly similar to the slang of today?? Amazing.) Shenanigans ensue with an extremely explicit song about lollipops. And every time Hannah (is there an H or no? Can’t remember), Ella and Nik have their lil instant-message conversations, my cold and bitter heart warms ever so slightly.<br><br>4. Total mind f*ck<br>There are some bad side effects to this bullet point, but also I spent most of the book like OH MAN WHAT IS GOING ON WHAT’S HAPPENING NEXT IS THIS REAL SCIENCE OR QUASI-SCIENCE EITHER WAY IT’S GOING OVER MY HEAD AND IT SOUNDS SMART SO I’M ALONG FOR THE RIDE. YOU GUYS JUST KEEP CRAWLIN’ THROUGH AIR VENTS AND PUNCHIN’ BAD GUYS.<br><br>5. It started off SO FREAKING WELL<br>I’ve been in an on-and-off reading slump for approximately 9 months, and when I first picked this up I wanted to do NOTHING BUT READ IT.<br>That honeymoon period faded.<br>But we’ll get there.<br>Ugh WHY DO THERE EVEN HAVE TO BE NEGATIVES TO THIS BOOK?!<br>I’ll let AnnaSophia Robb answer that:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499876090ra/23277110.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where is AnnaSophia Robb these days? Man, that girl has had a turbulent career. Her parts include a) tragic and traumatizing death in a children’s movie, b) alien, c) arm lost to shark.<br><br>Why do I keep talking about movies? I barely even like movies. I will force myself to move on.<br><br>It’s time to get into...THE BAD. (Insert ominous lightning bolt and thunder here, as if we are looking at a haunted house in a Scooby Doo cartoon.)<br><br><br><br><b>THE NOT SO GOOD</b><br><br>1. The...characters……….<br>Okay. So I know I just adoration-rambled about Ella for a hot Texas minute. This must be very confusing for you. I am sorry. <br>BUT ELLA IS THE ONLY CHARACTER WHO ACTUALLY EXISTS TO ME.<br>I found it totally impossible to connect to the actual main characters, Hannah (IS THERE AN H OR NOT) and Nik. Nik, in particular, was SO BORING. I felt like they were kind of just like “He is a bad boy. Here is his tragic backstory.” And then left it at that and hoped for the best. Hanna (I looked it up, no H) was similarly flat but less trope-y. Just somewhat nonexistent.<br>You can never have enough flat female protagonists!!!!!!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465484651ra/19363690.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>2. The...old characters………<br>If you have read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1829622315" rel="nofollow noopener">my Illuminae review</a>, you know that I hate Kady, the first book’s version of Hanna.<br>And guess who shows up pretty goddamn often?<br>If you guessed “that pink haired, defined-by-her-effortless-beauty identity-less buffoon,” you are correct.<br>If you guessed “said buffoon’s love interest, who Emma actually likes, and is charming and funny and has a - gasp! - personality,” you would, of course, be wrong.<br>Many generations ago, my ancestors betrayed the ancestors of every young adult author ever. The retribution is that I may never find literary happiness.<br>Also, AIDAN doesn’t feel as fun. (Insert whining noise here.)<br><br>3. ENOUGH ALREADY WITH THE LOVE FROM ALL SIDES<br>In Illuminae, I had to deal with the girl-so-effortlessly-beautiful-at-least-three-men-are-silently-pining-away-just-ready-to-martyr-themselves-whenever-given-the-chance trope. Abundantly.<br>AND IT GODDAMN REAPPEARS IN THIS BOOK, TOO.<br>Hanna is dating the ~most handsome guy~ on the entire!! jump station. Nik, also pretty hot, supposedly, is just pinin’ away. Everyone in the whole effin’ universe knows she’s hot sh*t.<br>Yes, we get Ella, who isn’t described exclusively in terms of her heart-stopping, universe-shaking, wormhole-damaging beauty. But that still doesn’t mean I want an unbelievably gorgeous girl who just ~doesn’t know she’s beautiful~ in every flippin’ book.<br><br><br>4. TOO MUCH LOVE, PT 2<br>THERE’S SO MUCH ROMANCE IN THIS BOOK. And there was so much romance in Illuminae. And all signs point to an equally immense sh*t ton of lovin’ in Obsidio, the upcoming third book, too. <br>Romance is fine as a subplot. But I’m not here for some interstellar romancing. I just want some badassery…<i>in space.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446480567ra/16814826.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>5. THIS LOVE SUCKS: A Companion Novel to the “Too Much Love” Duology<br>So, at the beginning of this book, Hanna is getting it on with the aforementioned hunk-boyfriend. Nik is her drug dealer. Nik constantly sexually harasses her and repeatedly asks her out despite her consistent lack of interest. At one point, Hanna points out that Nik doesn’t know anything about her except that she’s pretty. And he’s like “aw :( yeah i guess u hot kween.”<br>And then she’s all, ok, kiss my face for the rest of the book.<br>Which...what? Am I supposed to find this CUTE? I am supposed to “““ship””” “““this”””???? Bleh. Just punch more bad guys, please.<br><br>6. Is this just Illuminae?<br>An unlikely romance. A file folder containing documents that delineate the attempts of a corporation to kill civilians, being presented in order to prosecute that corporation. A hot, badass girl. A hot, badass boy. AIDAN. An unnamed employee taking ““humorous”” notes on surveillance footage. Lots of quasi-science and bad guy killing. A really gross and unexpected biohazard to add a twist of fun.<br>Like, did I read the same book twice? And the third book will just be me reading it a third time?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499876090ra/23277111.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>7. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[This book sure contains a f*ck ton of emotional manipulation before sitting you down, dusting you off and telling you everything’s fine. Ella dies like fourteen f*cking times but she remains alive. Both Nik AND Hanna die but they’re ok, too. Like...the amount of death that occurs only for the characters to still be alive is pretty unreal. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>8. I love mild confusion!!!!<br>Luckily, I truly enjoy being constantly perplexed! I find a light dusting of befuddlement to be invigorating. Feeling utterly uncertain for 700 pages? Count me the hell in!<br><br>8. These people have GOT to be superheroes<br>For roughly three-quarters of this book, our three main characters (plus, like, 200 side characters), go without eating or sleeping. One (1) character uses a bathroom one (1) time. These fools are constantly sprinting and crawling and shooting and fighting and experiencing one emotional trauma after the next. But no, feel free to mention one sleepless night and hint at the ingestion of raw meat and call it a fictional day.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466999489ra/19538503.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>9. ok...and the formatting wasn’t perfect<br>I know most people love surveillance-footage guy, the unnamed dude (maybe just person? Can’t remember if the character’s gendered) who summarizes the video from security tapes.<br>I don’t love him, BECAUSE HE SHOWS UP ALL THE TIME IN THIS BOOK. I needed more formatting variety.<br>Also, they censor the curse words in this series. What was charming in Illuminae is really distracting here. I don’t want to take 17 seconds every other page to try to analyze whether that blacked-out word is f*ck or sh*t.<br>And it’s not like the court documents of today black out curse words. Right?<br><br>10. One thing this review and this book have in common: they’re WAY TOO LONG<br>Gemina dragged. Not as bad as I’m sure this review is dragging, but still, man, it dragged.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499876090ra/23277112.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Bottom line: This was a very strange experience. I have no clue what to rate it. Bits were four stars, even five, but also three and two and one.<br><br>I guess I just have to give it that old placeholder rating of three stars.<br><br>Still read this book if you feel like it.<br><br><br><br><br><br>-----------------<br>currently-reading updates<br>-----------------<br><br>what is it about these books that prevents me from liking the characters?? storytelling-wise, plot-wise, creativity-wise, all fully brill. then when it comes to the characters, i am asleep. because i am bored. because i do not care. my lack of shits to give is preventing me from staying awake.<br><br>------------------<br><br>whoa.<br><br>this is already, like, a million times better than just-pretty-good illuminae.<br><br><s>but can these bozos write a female protagonist who isn't getting heart eyes from all sides??? bo-ring</s></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2364491950" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2364491950" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2364491950?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2364491950" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14921125203167156065"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1524939613ra/25449048.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> „War does not determine who is right <br/>- only who is left.“ </i> <br/><br/>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/>Did you ever think about the theory that our reality exist of many universes? <br/>That maybe, in another universe, you’re not a reader (😱) but a gamer or something else. <br/>There’s another version of you, or two or three. <br/>I need to say, that I’m probably not that smart that I could actually explain you this theory, but in this book this theory is called Gemina. <br/>(Like the freakin book.)<br/>Beitech did some real sh*t on Karenza (we can</span>
  <span id="freeText14921125203167156065" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1524939613ra/25449048.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> „War does not determine who is right <br>- only who is left.“ </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Did you ever think about the theory that our reality exist of many universes? <br>That maybe, in another universe, you’re not a reader (😱) but a gamer or something else. <br>There’s another version of you, or two or three. <br>I need to say, that I’m probably not that smart that I could actually explain you this theory, but in this book this theory is called Gemina. <br>(Like the freakin book.)<br>Beitech did some real sh*t on Karenza (we can all agree to that when we recall what happened in illuminae) and it didn’t stop after this. <br>No, no, no. <br>These f*ckers secretly creeped into Heimdall station and did a mess there too. <br>With a whole killer squad. (I actually thought this was a pretty cool group) <br>But they didn’t expect a badass blonde and a kind-of-dumb-but-pretty-cute criminal to cross their ways. <br>Oh, and a genius computer hacker with a big mouth and some seriously awesome humor. <br>I liked the story, the characters and the way this book was in the same special as Illuminae was. <br>But... (there’s always a but isn’t there?)<br>But I didn’t like the sequel as much as I loved the first book. <br>It was good, it was entertaining, but I missed my genius Aidan and his interactions with Kady. <br>So... I liked it. But it wasn’t worth 5 stars. <br>For all the hyper-fans out there: (don’t hate me, please?) I still continue with this series (I mean, I bought Obsidio with the rest of the books and it’s gorgeous) and it’s still one hell of a special and cool series that I’ll recommend everyone that needs “something different”. <br><br>Characters ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> „AIDAN: The concept of fortune is nonsensical, but Kady is insisting I wish you both good luck anyway.<br>AIDAN: So good luck, Hanna Donnelly.<br>AIDAN: The universe itself depends on you.<br>AIDAN: ...No pressure.” </i> <br><br>Did I mention that I missed my baby Aidan? There wasn’t enough Aidan time in my opinion. I want more, more, more. <br>But I was pretty satisfied with the replacements. Hanna donelly was a gorgeous badass with great physical strength and tactical talent. <br>You could say she probably saved some a*ses on Heimdall. <br>And Nik - my cutie pie - he had some strong really sweet parts in this book, that I loved. (Hint: flowers and cigarettes) <br>But even though I really liked all the characters mentioned in this book, i didn’t really feel them. You know what I mean? <br>I didn’t think of them in my free time apart from the book. I wasn’t sad or happy or something else. I felt pretty cold reading about them and that’s a pretty sad thing. <br>But... I liked Ella with her big mouth and her huge skills. She reminded me a lot of Kady with the Hacker vibe and the great dialogues. <br><br>World ⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> “Patience and Silence had one beautiful daughter. And her name was Vengeance.” </i> <br><br>Spaceships, killer operations, artificial intelligences, alien-things-that-suck-your-blood and different universes. <br>I wasn’t as excited about the sci-fi part in this book as I was with illuminae. <br>But it was still good, still exciting.<br>I actually really liked the whole killer squad thing. And all the twists and turns that appeared throughout the mission. <br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><i> „I cannot help but wonder<br>If the thought of saving all those lives and hopes and dreams <br>Pales in comparison<br>To the thought of seeing him again.<br><br>I wonder.” </i> <br><br>This was my least favorite part of the whole book. <br>Don’t get me wrong, I loved the two characters involved, they were pretty cute together. <br>But (always a but, ugh) <br>but for me it didn’t feel right. It was so fast and it had some love triangle parts in it, that I didn’t really like. <br>So. I’m sad, but okay with it. <br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>I loved the whole style in illuminae, but in Gemina it was different. It wasn’t something new anymore, I didn’t feel the excitement that I felt while reading Illuminae. <br>It was still pretty good, entertaining and interesting. But I was a little bit annoyed by some parts (like the parallel things). <br>Still I love the irony and sarcasm and the badass parts in this whole book! <br>Amy and Jay are pretty talented with that! <br>It’s still one of the most special books I have ever read and probably ever will and that’s why I’m not sad that I didn’t love this as much as I loved Illuminae, because that means that there’s still a huge possibility that I’ll love Obsidio (that I already have in my hands while finishing this review). <br>So. Fingers crossed guys! 💪🏻<br><br><i> „Her eyes shining with the light of it. <br>Beneath, between, beyond.<br>Along the endless circle.<br>Down the ceaseless spiral.<br>And waiting for her on the other side? <br>Just like he promised.<br>...<br>“A whole sky of different stars.” </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14921125203167156065" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2861368229" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2861368229" />
    <a title="megs_bookrack" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48328025-megs-bookrack"><img alt="megs_bookrack" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532027727p2/48328025.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2861368229?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="megs_bookrack" class="user" itemprop="url" name="megs_bookrack" href="/user/show/48328025-megs-bookrack">megs_bookrack</a>
      </span>

        rated it

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2861368229" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18359092199545528665"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487360957ra/22005187.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Soooooo, I am considering rereading this before I pick up <i>Obsidio</i>.   <span id="freeText18359092199545528665" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1487360957ra/22005187.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Soooooo, I am considering rereading this before I pick up <i>Obsidio</i>. In an unpopular opinion turn of events, I listened to the audiobook of this the first time round and wasn't crazy about it.<br><br>I feel like I want to read my hard copy before continuing on with the series, but it's a big book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1532978031ra/26052208.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>OPINIONS WANTED:</b> Should I try again with this or just roll on to <i>Obsidio</i>?<br><br><b>**3.5-stars**</b><br><br>In the second installment of <i>The Illuminae Files</i>, the BeiTech assault continues and we follow two all-new characters aboard the Jump Station <i>Heimdall</i>. <br><br>For those of you familiar with this series, you may recall that after the Kerenza attack, Kady Grant, aboard the <i>Hypatia</i>, was trying to reach the <i>Heimdall</i>. That was her hopeful destination.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577665112ra/28686133.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If this doesn't sound familiar, you most likely haven't read <i>Illuminae</i> yet. <br><br>To which I say...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1589072006ra/29446108.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you are interested, you can read my review here to see how much I loved it: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2082636385" rel="nofollow noopener">Meg's Illuminae Review</a><br><br>One thing you may be wondering by this point: why did I give this one only 3.5-stars, when I gave <i>Illuminae</i> ONE MILLION STARS?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1566333762ra/28023884.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Format. It's all about the format.<br><br>Due to receiving a lot of comments that I should try the audiobooks for this series, in conjunction with the hard copies, I decided to try it out. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1532809461ra/26044079.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was going on a long road trip, so downloaded the audiobook and additionally, packed my hard copy. <br><br>The thought was I could listen to the audio in the car and then while at our destination, I could read the hard copy.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577665112ra/28686134.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However, I had <u>zero time</u> to read on vacation...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501082663ra/23415525.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...so, I ended up listening to the entire thing on audio. <br><br>Now don't get me wrong, the production was flipping fantastic. Absolutely phenomenal full cast with sound effects, etc., but I am such a visual person, I missed the unique formatting and illustrations within the hard copy. <br><br>Thus, my heart didn't quite scream with joy as it did with the first book.<br><br>Additionally, I became quite attached to Kady, Ezra and AIDAN in <i>Illuminae</i> and was sad not to be following them directly in this story.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449304662ra/17265265.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I did eventually come to really enjoy Nik, the <i>Heimdall's</i> resident bad boy with a heart of gold and Hanna, its spoiled princess with an edge, but Kady will always be my number one.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1581172404ra/28926344.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is no doubt that this book is action-packed and a great continuation of the BeiTech assault. <br><br>I am really looking forward to the final book in the trilogy, <i>Obsidio</i>, but I will definitely be reading my hard copy version to conclude the series.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469047916ra/19775191.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1883091198" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1883091198" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1883091198?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780553499155" href="/book/show/29236298-gemina">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Melanie by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/42130592-chai">chai ♡</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=signed">signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1883091198" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10956402212014139573"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1519503736i/25117008._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1879957563' rel='nofollow noopener'>Illuminae</a> ★★★★<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Patience and Silence had one beautiful daughter. And her name was Vengeance.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>You all, I just don’t know what to say. This series just doesn’t do for me what it does for everyone else. I don’t dislike these books at all, they just aren’t even close to being one of my all time favorites either. Please, take this review with a grain of salt, because literally all of my friends five star this series. And even though I really like and appreciate the unique formatting, w</span>
  <span id="freeText10956402212014139573" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1519503736i/25117008._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1879957563" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a> ★★★★<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Patience and Silence had one beautiful daughter. And her name was Vengeance.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>You all, I just don’t know what to say. This series just doesn’t do for me what it does for everyone else. I don’t dislike these books at all, they just aren’t even close to being one of my all time favorites either. Please, take this review with a grain of salt, because literally all of my friends five star this series. And even though I really like and appreciate the unique formatting, witty banter, and twists and turns, I really hated to plot twist towards the end of this one. <i>*dodges tomatoes*</i> <br><br><i>Gemina</i> picks back up after the events of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1879957563" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a> and after that cliffhanger, jaw dropping, ending. But <i>Gemina</i> is set on Jump Station <i>Heimdall</i> which the ships in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1879957563" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a> were trying to get to. Also, this follows a whole brand-new set of characters who are living on this jump station. Yet the distinctive and special formatting is still there and is still how the story is told. I will say that <i>Gemina</i> also spends a little more time using surveillance cameras as a way for the reader to see, way more than of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1879957563" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a> did, too. <br><br>The main characters we follow on the <i>Heimdall</i> jump station:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1519766650i/25133704._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➽ <b>Hanna</b> - Daughter of the jump station’s commander. Also, a very good fighter, and very fast thinker, and a very talented artist. I loved seeing the story through her artwork, and it was for sure one of the highlights for me. (See picture above!) <br><br>➽ <b>Nik</b> - Heir to the House of Knives, drug dealer, and he has served time and has a tattoo to prove it. He is basically that typical “bad boy” which makes a good and angsty juxtaposition for Hanna’s “good girl” demeanor. <br><br>➽ <b>Ella</b> - Nik’s very computer savvy cousin, who helps them immensely through the entire book. She’s, hands down, the reason good things happened, and she was easily my favorite character. Also, she does all this while in a wheelchair and with an oxygen mask. Seriously, I love her and she is such a badass.<br><br>These three make up a fun YA SFF tale that is seamlessly woven and is quickly consumable and readable. Seriously, this 600+ page book felt like 250+ tops! And this was a fun read for me, that I feel so thankful that I was able to experience, especially with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2303028540" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidio</a> coming out in a couple of weeks. But sadly, I did have a few critiques. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I cannot help but wonder if his desire to see this place ripped to pieces pales in comparison to his desire to see her again.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The humor got to be too much. Like, I totally understand that everyone copes with intense situations very differently. And I’m completely aware that many people would use humor, but literally every single person in this uses humor and it got to be so over the top and unrealistic. On top of the fact that all of these people are around eighteen. Like, Lord, I couldn’t do it. What started out funny and cute ended up feeling like I was getting beat over the head and impractical.<br><br>Okay, let’s talk about the plot twist as vague as possible. I hate this plot twist. And the way that it was done in <i>Gemina</i> felt cheap, and it felt really exploitative of the readers emotions. This was a four star book for me up until a death didn’t happen. For me, it was a bad reading experience and I was angry that I shed tears and was impressed that the authors weren’t scared “to go there.” Again, let me heavily emphasize that all my friends love this book and didn’t feel this way. But my review, my feelings, and it felt bad, man. <br><br>And even though I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1879957563" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a> two years ago, I still felt like this book just felt too much like <i>Gemina</i>. The characters are different, but they still somehow feel the same. The catastrophes are different, but they still somehow feel read the same. The plots are different, but they still somehow appear the same. <br><br>Overall, I really did have a good time reading this. I thought it was funny, and smart, and action packed. I just don’t love this series the same way as everyone else. But I promise, I’m in the minority. Don’t let me or this mediocre review stop you. I honestly believe these books are worth a chance. And you’ll learn very quickly if they are or aren’t for you. Also, so many of my friends have recommended the audiobooks to me. Sadly, I’m the worst audiobook reader on this planet, but I think that’s also a good tip if you’re looking to start this series! <br><br><b>Trigger/Content Warnings:</b> Violence, gore, death, death of a parent, death of a loved one, and very minor animal cruelty.<br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="10956402212014139573" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1919765378?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alyssa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alyssa" href="/user/show/56485897-alyssa">Alyssa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1919765378" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13128648225895162435"><b>1 MILLION STARS!</b><br/><br/><b>Rating:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br/><b>Lead Male Character:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br/><b>Lead Female Character:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars (Hanna) ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars (Ella)<br/><b>Plotline:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars <br/><b>Genre:</b> Si-fi, fantasy, adventure, thriller, a bit of romance, and a whole lot of craziness!<br/><b>Will I recommend this book to others?:</b> Fuck yeah!<br/><b>Will I reread this book?:</b> YES!<br/><b>Overall story summed up in one word:</b> PERFECTION!<br/><br/>So I Googled the definition of <i>perfect</i> and this is what came up:<br/><br/><b>per•fect</b><br/><br/><i>adjective</i><br/>/pərfik</span>
  <span id="freeText13128648225895162435" style="display:none"><b>1 MILLION STARS!</b><br /><br /><b>Rating:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br /><b>Lead Male Character:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br /><b>Lead Female Character:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars (Hanna) ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars (Ella)<br /><b>Plotline:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars <br /><b>Genre:</b> Si-fi, fantasy, adventure, thriller, a bit of romance, and a whole lot of craziness!<br /><b>Will I recommend this book to others?:</b> Fuck yeah!<br /><b>Will I reread this book?:</b> YES!<br /><b>Overall story summed up in one word:</b> PERFECTION!<br /><br />So I Googled the definition of <i>perfect</i> and this is what came up:<br /><br /><b>per•fect</b><br /><br /><i>adjective</i><br />/pərfikt/<br /><br />1. having all the required or desirable elements, qualities, or characteristics; as good as it is possible to be. <br />"she strove to be the perfect wife"<br /><i>synonyms: </i> ideal, model, without fault, faultless, flawless, consummate, quintessential, exemplary, best, ultimate, copybook, etc. <br /><i>examples:</i> <b>Gemina by Amie Kaufman and Jay Kristoff.</b> <br /><br />Tbh, I think I may have enjoyed this a <i>little</i> more than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a>. Lmao I started this back in January as a buddy read and for some <b>odd</b> reason, I got bored of the book and stopped reading it. Now, three whole freaking months later, I continue it again and <b>FUCKING LOVED IT!</b> I don't even know why I stopped reading it. Three months ago, Alyssa wasn't thinking straight. I finally got my senses together to continue. And, I'm so sorry to my friends that BR this with me! I apologize for ditching you and promise to not do it again! <br /><br />Ok, going on with my review: <br /><br /><b>IF YOU HAVEN'T READ THIS BOOK OR THIS SERIES YET, PICK IT UP. I WILL PRESSURE YOU INTO READING IT IF YOU HAVEN'T ALREADY. I SWEAR, THIS BOOK IS MY LIFE, GUYS. WITHOUT THIS BOOK, HELL I WOULDN'T EVEN BE HERE. THAT IS HOW MUCH THIS SERIES MEANS TO ME! NIK WILL FOREVER AND ALWAYS BE MY LITTLE PRECIOUS BABY. DON'T TAKE HIM AWAY FROM ME. HE IS MINE! MINE!</b> I kinda liked Falk too. Guys like him are my type, if you know what I mean ;) <br /><br />I'm done now. Have a nice day, y'all :D</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3696569674169529338"><i> Ultimate buddy read with my darling (but-not-really-darling-more-like-kinda-a-lot-crazy) squad, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1705037986?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sana</a> ♡ <a>Ry</a> ♡ <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1823127486?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Em</a> ♡ <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1694208276?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Luna</a> ♡ <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1481612685?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Prag</a> ♡ <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1760280300?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Caitlin</a> ♡ <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1784358311?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jenn</a> ♡ <br/><br/>^^Click their names to see their reviews - you won't regret, they're fabulous. ♡ ♡ </i><br/><br/><br/>I’ve just spent the entire day in another universe, excuse me while I try to reintegrate into real life. <br/><br/>To give a brief summary of my emotions: <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480481077i/21314911.jpg' width='300' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This series just got so much better, like <i> multiple folds better. </i><br/><br/><i> Gemina </i> continues the story of Illuminae, but from the other</span>
  <span id="freeText3696569674169529338" style="display:none"><i> Ultimate buddy read with my darling (but-not-really-darling-more-like-kinda-a-lot-crazy) squad, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1705037986?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Sana</a> ♡ <a>Ry</a> ♡ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1823127486?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Em</a> ♡ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1694208276?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Luna</a> ♡ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1481612685?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Prag</a> ♡ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1760280300?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Caitlin</a> ♡ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1784358311?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Jenn</a> ♡ <br><br>^^Click their names to see their reviews - you won't regret, they're fabulous. ♡ ♡ </i><br><br><br>I’ve just spent the entire day in another universe, excuse me while I try to reintegrate into real life. <br><br>To give a brief summary of my emotions: <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480481077i/21314911.jpg" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series just got so much better, like <i> multiple folds better. </i><br><br><i> Gemina </i> continues the story of Illuminae, but from the other side of the wormhole, with kicka*s, Captain’s daughter Hanna and (kinda) delinquent-belongs-to-a-criminal-family Nik. Now where I adored Kady and Ezra, I fell in love with Hanna and Nik.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477964287i/21013857._SY540_.png" width="300" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>^^Yes, that was included in the book *squeals* <br><br>I don’t even know how to describe this book. It’s phenomenal. It’s starling. It’s jarring. It’s though provoking. It’s witty. It’s spectacular. <br><br>And the plot twists, the damned plot twists that have me crying and laughing and crying and clutching onto each and every word harder.<br><br>Open your minds up for this one, kids, because there’s some serious physics that’s gonna get your brain fizzled. <br><br>Amie Kaufman did an absolutely stupendous job on the parallels. So many parallels, so flawlessly written. Parallels of universes, worlds, characters, it’s all molded so seamlessly. <br><br>But the ending. :) Damn, that ending – especially making me wait an <b> entire </b> year before releasing the next one!!! *chaotic screaming*<br><br>I know I’m making less sense in this review than I did in my <i> Illuminae </i> review (and let’s be honest here, that’s saying something) but I URGE you to read this book because I have read no other book comparable. (also it’s really late at night and I’m suffering from post-book-completion-hangover and I have a lot of emotions in my heart and I just can’t write coherently.)<br><br>Read it please??<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384373944ra/6860280.gif" width="230" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i> <b> “You might get only one shot. So shoot. You know who said that?”<br>The rifle clatters to the bloody floor.<br>“Hanna ****ing Donnelly. That’s who.” </b> </i><br><br><br>All the stars!!!</span>

<div id="review_2440970958" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2440970958" />
    <a title="Warda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30036082-warda"><img alt="Warda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593385153p2/30036082.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2440970958?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Warda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Warda" href="/user/show/30036082-warda">Warda</a>
      </span>

          added it


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32767458-gemina">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2440970958" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6005922815987808976">Chums, am I the only one that feels confused reading these books?!<br/><br/>I'm going to attempt to review it, because honestly, so far, my feelings towards this trilogy, is all over the place. To the point where I can't rate it, because I'm feeling so conflicted.<br/><br/><b>THE GOOD:</b><br/>- The characters are awesome. Kady, Ezra, Hanna and Nik. Oh, fuckin AIDAN. First time I've had feelings towards a damn inanimate object, what the hell.<br/>- The writing was just soooo much FUN (and experimental) to read. I loved the differen</span>
  <span id="freeText6005922815987808976" style="display:none">Chums, am I the only one that feels confused reading these books?!<br /><br />I'm going to attempt to review it, because honestly, so far, my feelings towards this trilogy, is all over the place. To the point where I can't rate it, because I'm feeling so conflicted.<br /><br /><b>THE GOOD:</b><br />- The characters are awesome. Kady, Ezra, Hanna and Nik. Oh, fuckin AIDAN. First time I've had feelings towards a damn inanimate object, what the hell.<br />- The writing was just soooo much FUN (and experimental) to read. I loved the different styles of writing and narratives we got. This could've potentially added to my current confused state though.<br /><br /><b>THE CONFUSION:</b><br />- I couldn't tell you what the book is about.<br />- The format the story is told in. As exciting and new as it might have been for me, this is not something I was used to. Going in, I was prepared that it wasn't written or printed in your conventional book style, but that awareness didn't help. <br />- The story just didn't flow and despite me having read some parts of this through audiobook, it didn't fully connect the dots for me. Am I stupid?<br />- It threw me off quite often, because I'm so used to a story flowing. Thus, it felt disjointed.<br />- TOO MUCH DAMN SPACEY SCIENCE! My brain and science are at war tbh. Have been since me youngun' days. It likes simple, not science. Some science it can tolerate though.<br />- After two books, I still can't say I'm in love with this series.<br /><br />This is what my brain is currently processing. I still can't make sense out of... everything. At this point, I'm completing the series just to complete it. Not because there is a fondness towards it, or that it actually ended on some kind of cliffhanger. Was that what it was? <br /><br />Jeezus, I give up.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6005922815987808976" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_30075662'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30075662-aurora-rising"><img alt="Aurora Rising (The Aurora Cycle, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1560056657l/30075662._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RS53xIp39fJ6bo9D9ZaGaDU1xJzjqCR9bR0fLu/lBhi1sGV6WWCB1zU4sylVkiYKAVqFdkXyGMnp6RRx6TKVuQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

<span id="freeTextContainer5438533041778870586">Amie Kaufman is a New York Times and internationally bestselling author of young adult fiction. Her multi-award winning work is slated for publication in over 30 countries, and is in development for film and TV. Raised in Australia and occasionally Ireland, Amie has degrees in history, literature, law and conflict resolution. She lives in Melbourne with her husband, their rescue dog, and an extrem</span>
  <span id="freeText5438533041778870586" style="display:none">Amie Kaufman is a New York Times and internationally bestselling author of young adult fiction. Her multi-award winning work is slated for publication in over 30 countries, and is in development for film and TV. Raised in Australia and occasionally Ireland, Amie has degrees in history, literature, law and conflict resolution. She lives in Melbourne with her husband, their rescue dog, and an extremely large personal library.<br /><br />You can sign up for her newsletter to see what she's working on, hear when she releases a new book, and be automatically entered for giveaways: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.eepurl.com/6Ya8j">www.eepurl.com/6Ya8j</a><br /></span>
